{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:36","updatedTime":"2021-04-15 02:15:36","title":"Farm Before Pharm Branding and Packaging Design","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/JG8LTmVfYbU/farm-pharm-branding-and-packaging-design","description":"Farm Before Pharm Branding and Packaging Design\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/farm-pharm-branding-and-packaging-design\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/hero_vivo.jpg\" width=\"600\" height=\"900\" alt=\"Farm Before Pharm Branding and Packaging Design\" title=\"Farm Before Pharm Branding and Packaging Design\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>04.12.21\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/madebyinvade\">invade design</a> shared a branding and packaging design project for <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/vivolivefood/\">Vivo</a> a Medellín-based restaurant which offers healthy preparations using ingredients that were very carefully planted and harvested, from seed to crop to then be transported to the city. According to its owners, the food’s origin is the key to health, and that is why they decided to grow their ingredients in <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/vivolivefarm/\">their farm</a> in order to guarantee their traceability and thus to be able to strengthen the restaurant's value proposition.</p>\n\n<p>While designing their logo, the designer over at <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/madebyinvade\">invade design</a> saw a great opportunity to recreate plants growing from the soil, which allowed us to communicate the brand’s essence in a very effective way. Vivo promotes the origin but also goes beyond in terms of aesthetics, with blocks of warm and energetic colors. This idea also transpires in the dishes, decorated with edible flowers.</p>\n\n<blockquote>\n<p>We managed, through design, to transport an idea from the farm to the table, preserving the countryside while taking it to the city, where an audience can easily process it. As a brand, Vivo stands out for the simplicity of its message, and for its great effort in selecting ingredients.</p>\n</blockquote>\n\n<div class=\"imgsGrid\"><img The world has stopped around you, just to admire a piece of her art. From its execution, your senses have been triggered and complementing the imaginable color combinations ready to be unleashed. Well that's the art of <a href=\"https://maalavidaa.com/\">Alycia Rainaud</a>. She is a french graphic designer and digital art based in Montréal, Canada. My hometown! Her work is really focused on her journey through life's complexity through abstract art filled with hallucinogenic colors. She has entered the NFT space and she has been doing tremendously well. Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/plusx\">Plus X </a>has a connotation of the message that “We Add Experience for Your Brand.” Brand experience design means providing consumers with valuable brand experience through consolidated online and offline designs based on the consistent brand strategy. They believe that key brand messages or service functions can be effectively delivered when various media channels meet strategic marketing. That is visible in the mobile web UX/UI, web design and user experience work created for Neker.</p>\n\n<p>Launched in September 2020, Neker is a new cosmetics brand that strives to communicate with customers and the world, respecting diverse beauty and individual uniqueness. </p>\n\n<p><q class=\"pullquote\">Brand experience design means providing consumers with valuable brand experience through I remember doing a similar effect back in the day when I used to play and write tutorials every week so I decided to create a simple example this time using Pixelmator Pro, my photo editor of choice for speedy workflow (it’s so fast) - plus the non-destructive elements are game changer.</p>\n\n<p>I assume there are tons of ways to achieve the result, also you can make it more or less blurred, but here’s my simple or as Ryan asked “sneaky and clever” way.
